understood less, and sometimes he understood bits, and sometimes he understood nothing, as now. \n \nII \nWatt’s way of advancing due east was to turn his bust as far as possible towards the north and at the same time to fling his right leg as far as possible towards the south, and then to turn his bust as far as possible towards the south and at the same time to fling his left leg as far as possible towards the north, and then to turn his bust as far as possible towards the north and at the same time to fling his right leg as far as possible towards the south, and then again to turn his bust as far as possible towards the south and at the same time to fling his left leg as far as possible towards the north, and then again to turn his bust as far as possible towards the north and at the same time to fling his right leg as far as possible towards the south, and then once again to turn his bust as far as possible towards the south and at the same time to fling his left leg as far as possible towards the north, and then once again to turn his bust as far as possible towards the north and at the same time to fling his right leg as far as possible towards the south, and then yet again to turn his bust as far as possible towards the south and at the same time to fling his left leg as far as possible towards the north, and so on, over and over again, many many times, until he reached his destination, and could sit down. \nHis way of advancing due southeast was to turn his bust as far as possible towards the northeast and at the same time to fling his right leg as far as door locked, Watt went to the side door. \nFinding the side door locked, Watt went to the trapdoor. \nFinding the trapdoor locked, Watt went to the front door. \nFinding the front door locked, Watt returned to the back door. \nFinding the back door locked, Watt returned to the side door. \nFinding the side door locked, Watt returned to the trapdoor. \nFinding the trapdoor locked, Watt returned to the front door. \nFinding the front door locked, Watt again returned to the back door. \nFinding the back door locked, Watt again returned to the side door. \nFinding the side door locked, Watt again returned to the trapdoor. \nFinding the trapdoor locked, Watt again returned to the front door. \nFinding the front door locked, Watt once more returned to the back door. \nFinding the back door locked, Watt once more returned to the side door. \nFinding the side door locked, Watt once more returned to the trap- door. \nFinding the trapdoor now open, Watt was able to enter the house. \n \nIV
